\int{{\frac{3 \, x - 5}{{\left(x + 1\right)}^{2} {\left(x - 7\right)}^{2}}}\;dx} = \answer{{-\frac{x + 9}{8 \, {\left(x^{2} - 6 \, x - 7\right)}} + \frac{1}{64} \, \log\left(x + 1\right) - \frac{1}{64} \, \log\left(x - 7\right)}+C}
\]
\end{problem}}%}
